# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the API server admission webhook chain: the webhook admission controller, the webhook call dispatch, and the admission response aggregation.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the domain domain.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

Perfect! I've successfully identified and documented all the Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the API server admission webhook chain. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Components Identified:

### **Core Architecture Files (11 files)**
1. **Generic Webhook Controller** - `generic/webhook.go` - The base admission webhook with dispatcher integration
2. **Webhook Dispatcher Interface** - `generic/interfaces.go` - Defines Dispatcher, Source, and WebhookInvocation interfaces
3. **Mutating Webhook Plugin** - `mutating/plugin.go` - Plugin wrapper for mutating webhooks
4. **Mutating Dispatcher** - `mutating/dispatcher.go` - Implements sequential webhook invocation with patch application
5. **Validating Webhook Plugin** - `validating/plugin.go` - Plugin wrapper for validating webhooks
6. **Validating Dispatcher** - `validating/dispatcher.go` - Implements parallel webhook invocation
7. **AdmissionReview Handler** - `request/admissionreview.go` - Creates and verifies admission requests/responses
8. **Webhook Accessors** - `webhook/accessors.go` - Abstracts webhook configuration access
9. **Plugin Initializer** - `initializer/initializer.go` - Handles plugin setup
10. **Reinvocation Context** - `mutating/reinvocationcontext.go` - Tracks webhook re-invocation state
11. **Admission Chain Handler** - `chain.go` - Orchestrates the complete admission handler chain

### **Key Functionality Implemented:**
- **Webhook Dispatch**: Both sequential (mutating) and parallel (validating) dispatch patterns
- **Request/Response Handling**: Full AdmissionReview object creation and response verification
- **Patch Application**: JSON patch application for mutating webhooks
- **Webhook Re-invocation**: Context management for re-invoking webhooks when mutations occur

The `callHook()` method calls individual validation webhooks, and errors are collected and returned.
